ota-4.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn80@2020_6/2020/12/11/08-01-49-632_f2fc5a69072ae19e.webp","https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/photoshop-adjustment-layers-mask-edited.png?resize=876%2C560&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn30@2020_1/2020/12/11/08-01-49-235_263b2616ed8522b8.webp","https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/photoshop-adjustment-layers-options.png?resize=876%2C560&ssl=1":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn90@2020_1/2020/12/11/08-01-50-384_d2ea8afdd0d4528f.webp","https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/photoshop-adjustment-layers-leaf-bw.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&ssl=1":null,"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/DigitalPhotographySchool?i=AiwXu9Vwd8I:wv68VZn2X3w:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx31/cdn46@2020_5/2020/12/11/08-01-50-125_036cf642a7f6ba26.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/DigitalPhotographySchool?d=7Q72WNTAKBA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn22@2020_6/2020/12/11/08-01-51-829_849a6e90690e7208.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/DigitalPhotographySchool?d=ByNYXvuKCJE":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn44@2020_3/2020/12/11/08-01-48-226_7752f86734b1d8c8.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/DigitalPhotographySchool?i=AiwXu9Vwd8I:wv68VZn2X3w:guobEISWfyQ":null,"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/DigitalPhotographySchool/~4/AiwXu9Vwd8I":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn75@2020_6/2020/12/11/08-01-50-848_a8e1f67d128965eb.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1607673645670},{"createdTime":"2020-12-11 16:00:45","updatedTime":"2020-12-11 16:00:45","title":"10 Ways to Take Stunning Portraits","link":"https://digital-photography-school.com/10-ways-to-take-stunning-portraits/","description":"<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/10-ways-to-take-stunning-portraits/\">10 Ways to Take Stunning Portraits</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. It was authored by <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/author/darren/\">Darren Rowse</a>.</p>\n\n<p>How do you <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-take-portraits-19-portrait-photography-tutorials/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"take portraits (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">take portraits</a> that have the <em>wow </em>factor?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Today, I want to talk about taking portraits that are a little<strong> out of the box</strong>. You see, it&#8217;s all well and good to have a portrait that <strong>follows all the rules</strong> &#8211; but it recently hit me that <strong>often the most striking portraits are those that break the rules</strong>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"996\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=996%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"stunning portrait\" class=\"wp-image-198535\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?w=996&#38;ssl=1 996w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=199%2C300&#38;ssl=1 199w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=398%2C600&#38;ssl=1 398w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=768%2C1157&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=717%2C1080&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 996px) 100vw, 996px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>I want to look at some ways to break out of the mold and take <strong>striking portraits</strong> by breaking (or at least bending) the rules and by adding a little randomness to your <strong>portrait photography</strong>.</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"alter-your-perspective\">1. Alter your perspective</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Most portraits are taken with the camera at (or around) the eye level of the subject. While this is good common sense, completely changing the <a aria-label=\"angle that you shoot from (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/perspective-photography-dont-just-stand-move-feet/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">angle that you shoot from</a> can give your portraits a real <em>wow </em>factor.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1159\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-1.jpg?resize=1500%2C1159&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"stunning portrait high perspective\" class=\"wp-image-198526\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-1.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-1.jpg?resize=300%2C232&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-1.jpg?resize=600%2C464&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-1.jpg?resize=768%2C593&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-1.jpg?resize=717%2C554&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/get-a-new-perspective-by-getting-high/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Get up high</a> and shoot down on your subject, or <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/7-tips-for-great-low-angle-shots/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">get as close to the ground as you can and shoot up</a>. Either way, you&#8217;ll be seeing your subject from an angle that is bound to create interest.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1000\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-2.jpg?resize=1000%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"stunning portrait shooting from low down\" class=\"wp-image-198527\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-2.jpg?w=1000&#38;ssl=1 1000w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-2.jpg?resize=200%2C300&#38;ssl=1 200w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-2.jpg?resize=400%2C600&#38;ssl=1 400w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-2.jpg?resize=768%2C1152&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-2.jpg?resize=717%2C1076&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"play-with-eye-contact\">2. Play with eye contact</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>It is amazing how much the direction of your subject&#8217;s eyes can impact an image. Most portraits have the <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/eye-contact-smiles/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">subject looking down the lens</a> &#8211; something that can create a real sense of connection between a subject and those viewing the image. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>But there are a couple of other things to try:</p>\n\n\n\n<p><strong>A.</strong> <strong>Looking off-camera.</strong> <span style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Have your subject focus their attention on something outside the field of view of your camera. This can create a feeling of candidness and also create a little intrigue and interest as the viewer of the shot wonders what the subject is looking at. This intrigue is particularly strong when the subject is showing some kind of emotion (i.e., &#8220;What&#8217;s making them laugh?&#8221; or &#8220;What is making them look surprised?&#8221;). Just be aware that, when you have a subject looking out of the frame, you can also draw the eye of the viewer to the edge of the image, and this will take them away from the point of interest in your shot: the subject.</span></p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1385\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-3.jpg?resize=1385%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"subject looking off-camera\" class=\"wp-image-198528\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-3.jpg?w=1385&#38;ssl=1 1385w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-3.jpg?resize=277%2C300&#38;ssl=1 277w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-3.jpg?resize=554%2C600&#38;ssl=1 554w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-3.jpg?resize=768%2C832&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-3.jpg?resize=717%2C777&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p><strong><span style=\"font-weight: normal;\"><strong>B. Looking within the frame</strong></span></strong><span style=\"font-weight: normal;\">. </span><strong><span style=\"font-weight: normal;\">Alternatively, you could have your subject looking at something (or someone) within the frame. A child looking at a ball, a woman looking at her new baby, or a man looking hungrily at a big plate of pasta &#8211; it can all work. You see, when you give your subject something to look at that is inside the frame, you create a second point of interest and a relationship between it and your primary subject. It also helps create a story within the image.</span></strong></p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-4.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"woman looking at child stunning portrait\" class=\"wp-image-198529\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-4.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-4.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-4.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-4.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-4.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-4.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"break-the-rules-of-composition\">3. Break the rules of composition</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>There are a lot of &#8220;rules&#8221; out there when it comes to <a aria-label=\"composition (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/5-elements-of-composition-in-photography/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">composition</a>, and I&#8217;ve always had a love-hate relationship with them. My theory is that, while composition rules are useful to know and employ, they are also useful to know so you can purposely break them &#8211; as this can lead to eye-catching results.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The <a aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/rule-of-thirds/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">rule of thirds</a> is one rule that can be effective to break. You see, placing your subject dead-center can sometimes create a powerful image. And creative placement with your subject right on the edge of a shot can sometimes create interesting images.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1170\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-5.jpg?resize=1500%2C1170&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"stunning portrait centered\" class=\"wp-image-198530\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-5.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-5.jpg?resize=300%2C234&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-5.jpg?resize=600%2C468&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-5.jpg?resize=768%2C599&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-5.jpg?resize=717%2C559&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Another &#8220;rule&#8221; that we often talk about in portrait photography is to <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/give-your-subject-space-to-look-into/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">give your subject room to look into</a>. This can work really well &#8211; but again, sometimes rules are made to be broken.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1000\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-6.jpg?resize=1000%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"portrait with no room to look into\" class=\"wp-image-198531\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-6.jpg?w=1000&#38;ssl=1 1000w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-6.jpg?resize=200%2C300&#38;ssl=1 200w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-6.jpg?resize=400%2C600&#38;ssl=1 400w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-6.jpg?resize=768%2C1152&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-6.jpg?resize=717%2C1076&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"experiment-with-lighting\">4. Experiment with lighting</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Another element of randomness you can introduce in your portraits is the <a aria-label=\"way that you light them (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/6-portrait-lighting-patterns-every-photographer-should-know/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">way you light them</a>. There are almost unlimited possibilities when it comes to using light in portrait photography.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Sidelighting can create mood, while backlighting and <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-photograph-silhouettes/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"silhouetting your subject (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">silhouetting your subject</a> to hide their features can be powerful.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1000\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-7.jpg?resize=1000%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"sidelit portrait\" class=\"wp-image-198532\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-7.jpg?w=1000&#38;ssl=1 1000w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-7.jpg?resize=200%2C300&#38;ssl=1 200w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-7.jpg?resize=400%2C600&#38;ssl=1 400w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-7.jpg?resize=768%2C1152&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-7.jpg?resize=717%2C1076&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Also, using techniques like <a aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/slow-sync-flash/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">slow sync flash</a> (as well as <a aria-label=\"long exposures (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/step-by-step-guide-to-long-exposure-photography/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">long exposures</a> combined with <a aria-label=\"light painting (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/beginners-guide-to-light-painting/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">light painting</a>) can create impressive images.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-8.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"long exposure image with single flash\" class=\"wp-image-198533\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-8.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-8.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-8.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-8.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-8.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-8.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"move-your-subject-out-of-their-comfort-zone\">5. Move your subject out of their comfort zone</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>I was chatting with a photographer recently who told me about a corporate portrait shoot that he had done with a businessman at his home. They&#8217;d taken a lot of head and shoulder shots, shots at the desk, shots in front of framed degrees, and other &#8220;corporate&#8221; type images. The photos had all turned out fairly standard &#8211; but there was nothing that really stood out from the crowd.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The photographer and the subject agreed that there were plenty of usable shots, but they wanted to create something special and out-of-the-box. The photographer suggested they try some &#8220;jumping&#8221; shots. The subject was a little hesitant at first, but stepped out of his comfort zone &#8211; and then, dressed in his suit and tie, started jumping!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>The shots were amazing, surprising, and quite funny. The shoot culminated with the subject jumping into his pool for one last image!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>While this might all sound a little silly, the shots ended up being featured in a magazine spread about the subject. It was the series of out-of-the-box images that convinced the magazine the subject was someone they&#8217;d want to feature.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1000\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-9.jpg?resize=1000%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"man jumping\" class=\"wp-image-198534\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-9.jpg?w=1000&#38;ssl=1 1000w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-9.jpg?resize=200%2C300&#38;ssl=1 200w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-9.jpg?resize=400%2C600&#38;ssl=1 400w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-9.jpg?resize=768%2C1152&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-9.jpg?resize=717%2C1076&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"shoot-candidly\">6. Shoot candidly</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Sometimes, posed shots can look somewhat&#8230;posed. Some people don&#8217;t look good in a posed environment, and so switching to a <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/11-tips-for-better-candid-photography/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">candid-type approach can work well</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Photograph your subject at work, with family, or doing something that they love. This will put them more at ease, and you can end up getting some special shots with your subject reacting naturally to the situation they are in. You might even want to grab a longer zoom lens to give your subject space and get really &#8220;paparazzi&#8221; with them.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>I find that this can work particularly well when <a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/authentic-photos-children-simple-tips/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\"photographing children (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">photographing children</a>.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"996\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=996%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"candid child image\" class=\"wp-image-198535\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?w=996&#38;ssl=1 996w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=199%2C300&#38;ssl=1 199w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=398%2C600&#38;ssl=1 398w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=768%2C1157&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-10.jpg?resize=717%2C1080&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 996px) 100vw, 996px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"introduce-a-prop\">7. Introduce a prop</h3>\n\n\n\n<p><a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/props-are-evil-how-to-use-them-for-good/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Add a prop</a> of some kind, and you create another point of interest that can enhance your shot.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Yes, you might run the risk of taking too much focus away from your main subject. But you can also really add a sense of story and place to the image that takes it in a new direction, and gives the person you&#8217;re photographing an extra layer of depth that they wouldn&#8217;t have had without the prop.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-11.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"portrait with gum and candy as a prop\" class=\"wp-image-198536\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-11.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-11.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-11.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-11.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-11.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-11.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"focus-on-one-body-part-and-get-close-up\">8. Focus on one body part (and get close up!)</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Use a lens with a long focal length, or get up close so that you can just photograph a part of your subject. Photographing a person&#8217;s hands, eyes, mouth, or even just their lower body can leave a lot to the imagination of the viewer.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Sometimes, it&#8217;s what is left out of an image that says more than what is included.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1000\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-12.jpg?resize=1500%2C1000&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"woman's arm in field\" class=\"wp-image-198538\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-12.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-12.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-12.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-12.jpg?resize=768%2C512&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-12.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-12.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"obscure-part-of-your-subject\">9. Obscure part of your subject</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>A variation on the idea of zooming in on one part of the body is to obscure parts of your portrait subject&#8217;s face or body. You can do this with clothing, objects, your subject&#8217;s hands, or just by framing part of them out of the image.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Doing this means that you leave a little to the imagination of the viewer. And you also focus the viewer&#8217;s attention on the parts of your subject that you want focused on.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1038\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-13.jpg?resize=1500%2C1038&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"eyes stunning portrait\" class=\"wp-image-198539\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-13.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-13.jpg?resize=300%2C208&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-13.jpg?resize=600%2C415&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-13.jpg?resize=768%2C531&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-13.jpg?resize=717%2C496&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"take-a-series-of-shots\">10. Take a series of shots</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Switch your camera into <em>burst mode</em> (also known as <em><a href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/how-to-use-continuos-shooting-mode-on-a-digital-camera/\" target=\"_blank\" aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">continuous shooting mode</a></em>) and fire off several shots.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>In doing this, you create a series of images that could be presented together, instead of just one static image.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>This technique can work very well when you&#8217;re photographing children &#8211; or really when you&#8217;re photographing any active subject that is changing their position or pose in quick succession, like the runners below:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"791\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-999999.jpg?resize=1500%2C791&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"people running in a race\" class=\"wp-image-198540\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-999999.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-999999.jpg?resize=300%2C158&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-999999.jpg?resize=600%2C316&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-999999.jpg?resize=768%2C405&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/11/ways-to-take-stunning-portraits-999999.jpg?resize=717%2C378&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"ways-to-take-great-portraits-conclusion\">10 ways to take great portraits: conclusion</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Capturing stunning portraits is easy &#8211; as long as you remember a few of these simple tips! </p>\n\n\n\n<p>And if you&#8217;re interested in improving your portrait photography even further, make sure you&#8217;re <a aria-label=\" (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/subscribe/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">subscribed to the Digital Photography School newsletter</a>, where we share lots of photography tips and techniques every single week. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Also, make sure you check out the second half of this series here: <a aria-label=\"10 More Tips for Stunning Portrait Photography (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/tips-portrait-photography/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">10 More Tips for Stunning Portrait Photography</a>, as well as our <a aria-label=\"Portraits: Making the Shot (opens in a new tab)\" href=\"https://resources.digital-photography-school.com/download/portraits-book/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\" class=\"ek-link\">Portraits: Making the Shot</a> eBook!</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And start taking some great portraits, today!</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com/10-ways-to-take-stunning-portraits/\">10 Ways to Take Stunning Portraits</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"https://digital-photography-school.com\">Digital Photography School</a>. Tone Wheels, you can make both broad and targeted adjustments to the colors in your images. You can shift, brighten, and saturate colors selectively, you can push colors into the shadows, highlights, and midtones separately, and <em>so much more</em> &#8211; all with a few easy-to-use wheels and sliders. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>As someone who&#8217;s a bit color-obsessed, I&#8217;ve used quite a few color adjustment tools in many different post-processing programs. But I can honestly say that Photo Studio Ultimate&#8217;s version is one of the best implementations I&#8217;ve ever seen (if not <em>the </em>best). Yes, the wheels are amazingly powerful, and they should offer any amateur or professional all the color adjustment power they need. But they&#8217;re also just so fun and intuitive to work with, which is what&#8217;s really sold me on this program.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1436\" height=\"782\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-7.jpg?resize=1436%2C782&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"the Develop mode in ACDSee Photo Studio Ultimate 2021\" class=\"wp-image-200242\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-7.jpg?w=1436&#38;ssl=1 1436w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-7.jpg?resize=300%2C163&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-7.jpg?resize=600%2C327&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-7.jpg?resize=768%2C418&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-7.jpg?resize=160%2C88&#38;ssl=1 160w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-7.jpg?resize=717%2C390&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then open the Color Wheel panel on the left-hand side, and you&#8217;ll see a color wheel with a series of sliders below it:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"533\" height=\"1409\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-8.jpg?resize=533%2C1409&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"Color Wheel panel\" class=\"wp-image-200243\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-8.jpg?w=533&#38;ssl=1 533w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-8.jpg?resize=113%2C300&#38;ssl=1 113w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-8.jpg?resize=227%2C600&#38;ssl=1 227w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 533px) 100vw, 533px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Here&#8217;s what you need to know: </p>\n\n\n\n<p>The color wheel itself <strong>lets you select the colors you&#8217;re targeting in the photo</strong>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>And the sliders below it <strong>allow you to adjust the targeted colors</strong>. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So once you have your Color Wheel panel open, here&#8217;s what I recommend you do:</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-select-the-colors-you-want-to-adjust\">Step 1: Select the colors you want to adjust</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Selecting the colors you&#8217;d like to adjust pretty easy, and there are a couple of methods you can use. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>First, you can simply hover your cursor over different parts of your photo, and watch as it turns into a dropper icon:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"994\" height=\"1065\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-9.jpg?resize=994%2C1065&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"dropper tool\" class=\"wp-image-200244\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-9.jpg?w=994&#38;ssl=1 994w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-9.jpg?resize=280%2C300&#38;ssl=1 280w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-9.jpg?resize=560%2C600&#38;ssl=1 560w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-9.jpg?resize=768%2C823&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-9.jpg?resize=717%2C768&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 994px) 100vw, 994px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then, by clicking once on the photo, you&#8217;ll select that color for adjustment. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So if you click on a pinkish-purple part of your photo, you&#8217;ll select all the pink-purple colors:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"579\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-10.jpg?resize=1500%2C579&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"dropper example\" class=\"wp-image-200245\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-10.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-10.jpg?resize=300%2C116&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-10.jpg?resize=600%2C232&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-10.jpg?resize=768%2C296&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-10.jpg?resize=717%2C277&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And if you click on a yellow part of your photo, you&#8217;ll select all the yellow colors:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"825\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-11.jpg?resize=1500%2C825&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"dropper example\" class=\"wp-image-200246\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-11.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-11.jpg?resize=300%2C165&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-11.jpg?resize=600%2C330&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-11.jpg?resize=768%2C422&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-11.jpg?resize=620%2C340&#38;ssl=1 620w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-11.jpg?resize=160%2C88&#38;ssl=1 160w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-11.jpg?resize=717%2C394&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Now, as soon as you click on a part of your photo, you&#8217;ll see the color wheel change. This is to show you the color range you&#8217;ve selected.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You can also use the display on the color wheel to either <em>select</em> colors (instead of the eyedropper), or to <em>refine </em>your color selection.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>To select colors, just click on the relevant part of the wheel:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"513\" height=\"780\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-12.jpg?resize=513%2C780&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting a color on the color wheel\" class=\"wp-image-200247\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-12.jpg?w=513&#38;ssl=1 513w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-12.jpg?resize=197%2C300&#38;ssl=1 197w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-12.jpg?resize=395%2C600&#38;ssl=1 395w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 513px) 100vw, 513px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And to fine-tune the color selection, just narrow the range of colors on the color wheel &#8211; by dragging the edges of the selection inward or outward. That way, the adjustments you make via the sliders will affect a narrower or broader<em> </em>range of colors in your photo.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Here, I&#8217;ve narrowed the color selection:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"507\" height=\"750\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-43.jpg?resize=507%2C750&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"narrow selection on the color wheel\" class=\"wp-image-200248\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-43.jpg?w=507&#38;ssl=1 507w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-43.jpg?resize=203%2C300&#38;ssl=1 203w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-43.jpg?resize=406%2C600&#38;ssl=1 406w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 507px) 100vw, 507px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And here I&#8217;ve broadened it:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"496\" height=\"749\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-13.jpg?resize=496%2C749&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"broad selection on the color wheel\" class=\"wp-image-200249\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-13.jpg?w=496&#38;ssl=1 496w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-13.jpg?resize=199%2C300&#38;ssl=1 199w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-13.jpg?resize=397%2C600&#38;ssl=1 397w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 496px) 100vw, 496px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Also, if you want to get really picky with your selection, you can drag your color range upward from the center of the wheel:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"504\" height=\"753\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-14.jpg?resize=504%2C753&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting only saturated areas\" class=\"wp-image-200250\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-14.jpg?w=504&#38;ssl=1 504w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-14.jpg?resize=201%2C300&#38;ssl=1 201w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-14.jpg?resize=402%2C600&#38;ssl=1 402w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 504px) 100vw, 504px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And this will ensure you only select the more saturated colors.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>You can also drag downward from the rim of the wheel to select only the less-saturated colors:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"495\" height=\"744\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-15.jpg?resize=495%2C744&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"selecting only desaturated colors\" class=\"wp-image-200251\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-15.jpg?w=495&#38;ssl=1 495w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-15.jpg?resize=200%2C300&#38;ssl=1 200w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-15.jpg?resize=399%2C600&#38;ssl=1 399w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 495px) 100vw, 495px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>By the way, if you want to see the areas you&#8217;ve selected displayed on your photo, just hit the <strong>Auto preview the selected range </strong>checkbox:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"500\" height=\"731\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-16.jpg?resize=500%2C731&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"previewing the selection\" class=\"wp-image-200252\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-16.jpg?w=500&#38;ssl=1 500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-16.jpg?resize=205%2C300&#38;ssl=1 205w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-16.jpg?resize=410%2C600&#38;ssl=1 410w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Your selected colors will be highlighted on the image, while everything else will be grayed out:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"887\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-17.jpg?resize=1500%2C887&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"previewing the selection\" class=\"wp-image-200253\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-17.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-17.jpg?resize=300%2C177&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-17.jpg?resize=600%2C355&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-17.jpg?resize=768%2C454&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-17.jpg?resize=717%2C424&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Cool, right?</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-adjust-the-colors-using-the-sliders\">Step 2: Adjust the colors using the sliders</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>Now comes the fun part:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Actually adjusting the colors. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>While there are a number of sliders, I recommend you focus on three key options: </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Hue. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Saturation.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>And Brightness. </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"505\" height=\"745\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-18.jpg?resize=505%2C745&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"hue, saturation, and brightness sliders in ACDSee Photo Studio Ultimate 2021\" class=\"wp-image-200254\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-18.jpg?w=505&#38;ssl=1 505w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-18.jpg?resize=203%2C300&#38;ssl=1 203w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-18.jpg?resize=407%2C600&#38;ssl=1 407w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 505px) 100vw, 505px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>These are the main adjustments you&#8217;ll want to make (I use them on almost <em>every </em>photo I edit).</p>\n\n\n\n<p>By shifting the Hue slider, you shift the hue of your selected color range. So if I select the pink colors in this flower photo and want to make them more purple, I can just push the Hue slider to the left:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"998\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-44.jpg?resize=1500%2C998&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"shifting the hue\" class=\"wp-image-200255\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-44.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-44.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-44.jpg?resize=600%2C399&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-44.jpg?resize=768%2C511&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-44.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-44.jpg?resize=717%2C477&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>I can also make them more red by pushing the Hue slider to the right:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"999\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-19.jpg?resize=1500%2C999&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"shifting the hue\" class=\"wp-image-200256\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-19.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-19.jpg?resize=300%2C200&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-19.jpg?resize=600%2C400&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-19.jpg?resize=768%2C511&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-19.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-19.jpg?resize=717%2C478&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Speaking more generally, the Hue slider is useful for situations where you want to separate colors to create contrast, or where you want to make colors more similar to add harmony. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>(How do you know what creates contrast and what creates harmony? Look at the color wheel! Colors that are opposite one another are <em>contrasting/complementary </em>colors, whereas colors next to one another are <em>analogous </em>colors.)</p>\n\n\n\n<p>While color contrast will generally create a more powerful, in-your-face photo, analogous colors can result in a more peaceful final image. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Anyway, once you&#8217;ve adjusted the hue, I recommend turning to the Saturation slider. This works the way it sounds: It lets you selectively boost or reduce the saturation of your selected color range. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So by selecting the yellows in the image below, then adjusting the Saturation slider, you can boost the yellow intensity:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1029\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-20.jpg?resize=1500%2C1029&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"shifting the saturation\" class=\"wp-image-200257\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-20.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-20.jpg?resize=300%2C206&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-20.jpg?resize=600%2C412&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-20.jpg?resize=768%2C527&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-20.jpg?resize=717%2C492&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Or you can dial it back:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"1011\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-21.jpg?resize=1500%2C1011&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"shifting the saturation\" class=\"wp-image-200258\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-21.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-21.jpg?resize=300%2C202&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-21.jpg?resize=600%2C404&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-21.jpg?resize=768%2C518&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-21.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-21.jpg?resize=436%2C293&#38;ssl=1 436w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-21.jpg?resize=717%2C483&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>In general, boosting the saturation of your main colors looks pretty good, as long as you don&#8217;t overdo it. That way, a few colors in your photo will stand out and keep the viewer interested. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>However, it can also be helpful to reduce the saturation of colors that distract from the main subject. So if your photo includes a red &#8220;Exit&#8221; sign in the background, you might reduce the saturation of those reds to keep the viewer focused on the foreground. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Finally, I recommend experimenting with the Brightness slider. This allows you to adjust the brightness of your selected color range. So you can brighten up your selection to make it pop: </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"987\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-22.jpg?resize=1500%2C987&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"shifting the brightness\" class=\"wp-image-200259\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-22.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-22.jpg?resize=300%2C197&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-22.jpg?resize=600%2C395&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-22.jpg?resize=768%2C505&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-22.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-22.jpg?resize=115%2C75&#38;ssl=1 115w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-22.jpg?resize=717%2C472&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Or you can darken the selection down to make it less impactful:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"988\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-23.jpg?resize=1500%2C988&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"shifting the brightness\" class=\"wp-image-200260\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-23.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-23.jpg?resize=300%2C198&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-23.jpg?resize=600%2C395&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-23.jpg?resize=768%2C506&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-23.jpg?resize=90%2C60&#38;ssl=1 90w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-23.jpg?resize=115%2C75&#38;ssl=1 115w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-23.jpg?resize=717%2C472&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-create-additional-color-wheels-for-further-adjustments\">Step 3: Create additional color wheels for further adjustments</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>While one color adjustment may sometimes be enough, you also have the option to create more.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Simply click the <em>Plus </em>icon: </p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"502\" height=\"757\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-24.jpg?resize=502%2C757&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"adding color wheels\" class=\"wp-image-200261\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-24.jpg?w=502&#38;ssl=1 502w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-24.jpg?resize=199%2C300&#38;ssl=1 199w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-24.jpg?resize=398%2C600&#38;ssl=1 398w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 502px) 100vw, 502px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then follow the previous steps all over again! </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Also, to toggle the effects of the color wheels on and off, you can just check and uncheck the box above each color wheel icon:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"497\" height=\"744\" src=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-25.jpg?resize=497%2C744&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"viewing the effects of color wheels\" class=\"wp-image-200262\" srcset=\"https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-25.jpg?w=497&#38;ssl=1 497w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-25.jpg?resize=200%2C300&#38;ssl=1 200w, https://i2.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-25.jpg?resize=401%2C600&#38;ssl=1 401w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 497px) 100vw, 497px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<h2 data-section id=\"how-to-use-the-tone-wheels-to-produce-beautiful-color-grading\">How to use the Tone Wheels to produce beautiful color grading</h2>\n\n\n\n<p>The Tone Wheels panel is located just below the Color Wheel panel in the Develop<strong> </strong>mode of Photo Studio Ultimate 2021:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"463\" height=\"1500\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-26.jpg?resize=463%2C1500&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"using the tone wheels in ACDSee Photo Studio Ultimate 2021\" class=\"wp-image-200263\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-26.jpg?w=463&#38;ssl=1 463w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-26.jpg?resize=93%2C300&#38;ssl=1 93w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-26.jpg?resize=185%2C600&#38;ssl=1 185w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 463px) 100vw, 463px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Now, unlike the Color Wheel panel, you cannot select individual colors to adjust. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Instead, each of the three wheels corresponds to a different tonal range of your photo:</p>\n\n\n\n<ul><li>The top wheel corresponds to the highlights (the brightest tones)</li><li>The middle wheel corresponds to the midtones (the middle tones)</li><li>The bottom wheel corresponds to the shadows (the darkest tones)</li></ul>\n\n\n\n<p>And by adjusting the tone wheels, you change the color in the corresponding area of the image. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>So by setting the Highlights wheel to yellow, your photo&#8217;s highlights will be tinted yellow:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"778\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-27.jpg?resize=1500%2C778&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"adding yellow highlights\" class=\"wp-image-200264\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-27.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-27.jpg?resize=300%2C156&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-27.jpg?resize=600%2C311&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-27.jpg?resize=768%2C398&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-27.jpg?resize=717%2C372&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>And by setting the Shadows wheel to green, your photo&#8217;s shadows will be tinted green:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"764\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-28.jpg?resize=1500%2C764&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"adding green shadows\" class=\"wp-image-200265\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-28.jpg?w=1500&#38;ssl=1 1500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-28.jpg?resize=300%2C153&#38;ssl=1 300w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-28.jpg?resize=600%2C306&#38;ssl=1 600w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-28.jpg?resize=768%2C391&#38;ssl=1 768w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-28.jpg?resize=717%2C365&#38;ssl=1 717w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1000px) 100vw, 1000px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>This is a fantastic way to add different looks to your images. For instance, you can create blue shadows and yellow highlights, which is a popular look on Instagram. Or you can make the highlights orange and the shadows teal, for a cinematic, movie-type result.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now, the tone wheels themselves only allow you to select the hue and saturation of the color you&#8217;d like to add.</p>\n\n\n\n<p>But by shifting the Brightness slider &#8211; found to the right of each wheel &#8211; you can also make the highlights, midtones, and shadows brighter or darker.</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"503\" height=\"1035\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-29.jpg?resize=503%2C1035&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"the brightness sliders\" class=\"wp-image-200266\" srcset=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-29.jpg?w=503&#38;ssl=1 503w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-29.jpg?resize=146%2C300&#38;ssl=1 146w, https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-29.jpg?resize=292%2C600&#38;ssl=1 292w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 503px) 100vw, 503px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>So how do you get great results using the Color Wheel panel? How should you approach this color adjustment tool?</p>\n\n\n\n<p>Here&#8217;s what I recommend:</p>\n\n\n\n<h3 data-section id=\"step-adjust-the-shadows\">Step 1: Adjust the shadows</h3>\n\n\n\n<p>I like to start by adjusting the shadows in my images. </p>\n\n\n\n<p>Now, you can choose your shadow color a few different ways:</p>\n\n\n\n<p>One method is to select the Shadows eyedropper:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"500\" height=\"1020\" src=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-30.jpg?resize=500%2C1020&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"the shadows eyedropper\" class=\"wp-image-200267\" srcset=\"https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-30.jpg?w=500&#38;ssl=1 500w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-30.jpg?resize=147%2C300&#38;ssl=1 147w, https://i1.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-30.jpg?resize=294%2C600&#38;ssl=1 294w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px\" data-recalc-dims=\"1\" /></figure></div>\n\n\n\n<p>Then you can click on a part of your photo and the Shadows wheel will select its hue:</p>\n\n\n\n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"><figure class=\"aligncenter size-full\"><img loading=\"lazy\" width=\"1500\" height=\"632\" src=\"https://i0.wp.com/digital-photography-school.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/12/photo-studio-ultimate-tone-wheels-color-wheel-31.jpg?resize=1500%2C632&#038;ssl=1\" alt=\"picking a shadow color\"
